üîîService: Overall, the service is very good. After staying for nearly two months, I switched to the nearby Sheraton. It can be clearly felt that the former is a local 5-star hotel, while the latter is an international chain.
       Carnival's service process: Objectively speaking, there is no international chain that does it well. Especially on the issue of guest privacy, even if related issues have been reflected. After that, there will still be examples: because the cleaning cloth is missing, the cleaning aunt will come to knock on your door. Even if you tell her someone is taking a nap in bed. The aunt would still say "it's okay" while poking into the house to check. When you are busy outside, the front desk will keep calling you because of a piece of clothing "Do you need to send laundry?"
        Service content: Carnival does a good job. For example, the hotel insisted on delivering breakfast for more than a month. Every day at 8:30, it will be delivered on time, which is quite rare. Basically, all requests put forward by the hotel will be met as much as possible. This is something that Sheraton cannot do. In order to increase customer stickiness, those international chains have worked hard and considered all possible additional services as a condition for extending the customer's stay, so the flexible space for communication is actually very small.
       To sum up: the official price of Xiamen Airlines Carnival is more than 30% off compared to Sheraton. Although the service seems to be very localized, it varies from person to person. I think people in China may be more accustomed to living in it. Although the process of the hotel is poor, it can be communicated and there is a lot of room for negotiation. Management was quick to respond when issues arose, and the results were very good. Coupled with the hotel's very superior location, shopping or transportation are very convenient. Overall, it's worth staying in. I regretted it the day I changed hotels.
